\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_8cpp_source_l01987}01987\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Finding\ Newton\ direction:\ -\/inv(H')\ *\ g}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_8cpp_source_l01988}01988\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacenumpy_1_1array__api_1_1linalg_ac941222dff4db110e77348578dbd93a9}{det}}=h11*h22-\/h21*h21;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_8cpp_source_l01989}01989\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ dA=-\/(h22*g1\ -\/\ h21\ *\ g2)\ /\ det;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_8cpp_source_l01990}01990\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ dB=-\/(-\/h21*g1+\ h11\ *\ g2)\ /\ det;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_8cpp_source_l01991}01991\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ gd=g1*dA+g2*dB;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{svm_8cpp_source_l01992}01992\ }
